 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Road Rebel                                                    บ
 บ    Subject : Introduction to RCN #18                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am writing this to say a few words about RCN and how people treat   บ
 บ  us.  First of all, when you see an article that rips on someone or a      บ
 บ  group, and you don't like it.  Take it up with the author!!!  If it       บ
 บ  isn't written by Rebel Chicken, Hitex or I then don't nag us about it!    บ
 บ  Also, if you have a problem with something written about you or a group,  บ
 บ  WRITE A REBUTTLE!  Don't sit there and bitch at us in the channel, it     บ
 บ  doesn't do shit.  I came to #RCN today, and all I heard was bitching      บ
 บ  because someone said something mean about a group.  WELL, if you are a    บ
 บ  group member and your group gets made fun of, take it on the chin, be a   บ
 บ  man.  We have and will make fun of A LOT of people, most of it is just    บ
 บ  FUN and in MAD RCN, and people realize this and get over it.  If you      บ
 บ  come in and bitch at us, it makes us want to rip you some more.  Ok       บ
 บ  enough of this.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, this is for the people that come in and say "SEND ME THE NEWEST  บ
 บ  RCN!"  You don't have to beg!!!!  Before you nag people for it try this.  บ
 บ  Look in the channel for someone named *dcc (anythingdcc).  If they exist  บ
 บ  type this : "/MSG <nick> xdcc list"  If they list that they have it type  บ
 บ  this : "/MSG <nick> xdcc send #<pack@>"                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      OK!!  NOW, if there isn't a DCC in the channel look at the topic.     บ
 บ  It will usually have an FTP or Web page adrress!  If they aren't there,   บ
 บ  then ask.  Please don't just come in and BEG. It is very unbecoming.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also, for people that want to write for RCN, you don't have to ask    บ
 บ  for an RCN app.  Just write something and send it to me.  If it is good   บ
 บ  we use it, if not, well.. we don't.  However, our editors are very        บ
 บ  patient and they will try to unscramble any submission, regardless of     บ
 บ  your English skills.  Also, we readily accept submissions written in      บ
 บ  French, Hebrew, Spanish, or Swedish.  Don't worry, we'll get it           บ
 บ  translated!  (Of course, we still prefer English!)  If you can keep       บ
 บ  submitting to RCN you will become a member.  But don't ask what the       บ
 บ  topic should be, if we had all the topics we could write the whole        บ
 บ  magazine, the topics are the hard part!                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyways, I was almost busted last night.  I was emailed by the SPA    บ
 บ  saying their usual bullshit and then I was given a phone call by the      บ
 บ  RCMP telling me that I was guilty of carding and software piracy.         บ
 บ  Further more, they came to inspect my computer which I was wise enough    บ
 บ  to have deleted all my warez before hand, they checked me out and played  บ
 บ  a recorded voice of me when I was making some c00kies also know as        บ
 บ  calling cards.  Not sure how to end this but I was very close to getting  บ
 บ  my ass kicked, but I was only fined 5000 bucks, which still sux :(.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, I won't be back for a while, I might even be quitting the       บ
 บ  scene as a whole.  I'm gonna be thinking about it today.  Keep up the     บ
 บ  good work for RCN!!!                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Endokuken                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Endokuken,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you're reading this, just want to let you know that the scene      บ
 บ  will miss you.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear kT!,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Right now, I should be studying for my finals, and that is the        บ
 บ  reason for my not hanging around on IRC quite as much, but this letter    บ
 บ  that you wrote and submitted to RCN got me pissed and I when saw how      บ
 บ  WRONG you were, I HAD to write this.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First of all, who the FUCK are you!?  Why don't you use your fucking  บ
 บ  entire handle instead of kT so we know who you are?  Not that it makes a  บ
 บ  damn bit of difference, but I am curious.  I don't know exactly who you   บ
 บ  are, but I will keep guessing until you reply.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, let me tell you that our NFO is pretty damn good, and if   บ
 บ  you can do anything better, please do so and we will see how damn good    บ
 บ  it is.  About the "They have ripped off parts of DOD and PWA's NFOs."     บ
 บ  Let me tell you that I never ripped any of Razor's part of the NFO.  And  บ
 บ  I got PERMISSION from PWA, and DOD to take those certain arts of the NFO  บ
 บ  file and use it myself.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Second, you said "The only original statement is the group's quote    บ
 บ  and that this is one of hypocrisy. 'COPS will beat you and you will like  บ
 บ  it!'"  What is your problem?  This is our statement like many other       บ
 บ  groups have!  Take a break man!  We are not "FOR" police brutality, but   บ
 บ  I guess your ass doesn't see the satire in it.  It's a good statement,    บ
 บ  and we will keep it.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Third, you said "When a non-foreign group starts releasing software   บ
 บ  in another language, you know it is in trouble."  Let me tell you         บ
 บ  something.  A lot of people in the scene are not of American origin,      บ
 บ  like myself.  But I am not Chinese either.  I respect the others in the   บ
 บ  scene, and I don't take to my own selfish interest to release only US     บ
 บ  Warez.  There are MANY Asians in the scene, and it's MORE than 15%.       บ
 บ  COPS is not the ONLY group to release foreign warez.  Why don't you bash  บ
 บ  some other groups?  The MS Access in Chinese was a "quality foreign       บ
 บ  release" unlike some stupid release like "Mahwai Checkers" or something.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Fourth, you said "Also, when you released Blake Stone, you knew that  บ
 บ  the files dated back to 1993, yet you gave the go-ahead to release."      บ
 บ  WRONG!  I didn't know the release date of that game, because to tell you  บ
 บ  the truth, I have never heard of it before.  And the person that          บ
 บ  packaged it didn't want his identity to be revealed.  It was my mistake   บ
 บ  not to check the file dates, and yes, it was a "lame" release as you may  บ
 บ  call it, but that is the ONLY one that is ever gonna come out of COPS.    บ
 บ  I apologized for that release and I will do so again.  So enough said     บ
 บ  about that.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Fifth, you said "But then again, fATE is a second-rate couriering     บ
 บ  group."  Don't start bashing on fATE, because your stupid ass wasn't      บ
 บ  good enough to get in, even if you tried.  MALiCE is a GOOD couriering    บ
 บ  group, but the council members of that group were VERY poor and had a     บ
 บ  hard time managing.  And I am glad that they left.  MALiCE will probably  บ
 บ  do good without them, and hopefully become #2 again next to RiSC in the   บ
 บ  future.                                                                   บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I would like to start by clarifying what H/P/A/V/C actually refers    บ
 บ  to.  Believe it or not, this question has been asked of me numerous       บ
 บ  times while meddeling on IRC.  In H/P/A/V/C, H stands for Hacking, P      บ
 บ  stands for Phreaking, A stands for Anarchy, V stands for Virii, and C     บ
 บ  stands for Carding.  Those 5 things, my friends, are what made the        บ
 บ  "warez world" of today.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The abundance of people in the #WarezX channels that have asked me    บ
 บ  this question has lead me to understand how severely messed up the scene  บ
 บ  is today.  Let's take a trip back to the time when people with 300 baud   บ
 บ  modems and 20 megabyte hard drives were elite.  People didn't have        บ
 บ  enough space, nor interest, to trade 300 disk warez.  Heck, people        บ
 บ  didn't even trade warez, they traded H/P/A/V/C text and utils!  My point  บ
 บ  here is that no one in the scene knows about its roots!                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Before there were warez, there was H/P/A/V/C.  People who don't know  บ
 บ  about this should really take the time to learn.  I remember the days     บ
 บ  when Jolly Roger ruled the scene for text files on telling you            บ
 บ  everything from how to get free HBO to how to make Solidox Bombs.  I      บ
 บ  mean groups like BOM (Brotherhood of Malice) and BGR (Brotherhood of      บ
 บ  Gods and Retards) would put out text files every week for the average     บ
 บ  Joe Schmoe who didn't want to pay for that Porno Movie in the hotel or    บ
 บ  that Snickers bar in the candy machine.  The people who know what I am    บ
 บ  talking about are VERY lucky.  If you can recall some of the stuff I am   บ
 บ  saying please help me on my crusade to revive the scene.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What people have to understand is that there was no Internet when     บ
 บ  the scene started.  I mean, there was no IRC to trade 0 day warez on,     บ
 บ  there were only BBSes.  SLOW BBSes I might add.  There was actually       บ
 บ  talent and skill involved in making a black box so you could call long    บ
 บ  distance.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What has so angered me about the scene today is that the only thing   บ
 บ  people are interested in is 0-day Warez.  Okay, I admit that I LOVE       บ
 บ  warez, but when I see Mayo Family Clinic being couriered it's time to     บ
 บ  stop.  I mean, I understand someone couriering a good ware such as Duke   บ
 บ  Nukem 3D, but the QUALITY is what really counts not the QUANTITY.  At     บ
 บ  least, that's the way I see it.  Unfortunately, just about everyone else  บ
 บ  doesn't see it my way.  They are interested in how many warez they can    บ
 บ  courier in 1 day or how many releases they can put out.  This is wrong    บ
 บ  and needs to be stopped.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      One other thing that I can't stand is that every Joe BumFuck and his  บ
 บ  brother is creating little shit groups these days.  I can remember when   บ
 บ  art groups ruled the scene, and there were only a few people cool enough  บ
 บ  to start a group.  The IRC and the Internet as a whole have made it       บ
 บ  easier for little shitoids to start groups every 5 seconds.  The only     บ
 บ  groups I have respect for at the moment are big named groups such as      บ
 บ  fATE, DOD, Razor 1911, and PWA, because the reason they are "big names"   บ
 บ  is that many have heard them and they USUALLY release great, working      บ
 บ  warez.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The dismanteling of the scene has greatly upset me and many other     บ
 บ  "old timers" because the scene was SO much nicer once upon a time.  Was   บ
 บ  it better? I would say yes, but then I wouldn't be playing Duke Nukem     บ
 บ  3D!                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Bollox                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Bollox,                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I don't buy it.  The nature of man hasn't changed since 1986 and I    บ
 บ  won't believe it for a minute that the scene was ever any better.  Look   บ
 บ  you really couldn't have been too excited when you downloaded Pong for    บ
 บ  the Commodore 64, or leeched a file on how to get free change out of a    บ
 บ  vending machine.  And moreover, I won't believe for a minute that the     บ
 บ  scene wasn't just as fucked up in 1986 as it is now.  The only thing      บ
 บ  that's changed is the resources we have to work with, and that's an       บ
 บ  omnipresent change that will never go away.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Furthermore, the hacking scene is just as alive today as it was 10    บ
 บ  years ago.  NO, I take that back.  It's even MORE alive.  The only        บ
 บ  reason I can see for you not to be enjoying those great text files now    บ
 บ  is that perhaps you couldn't get on any of the boards on which these      บ
 บ  guys hang out.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'll skip the formalities, we all know that RCN is the best.  Before  บ
 บ  I start, I would like to say that I am writing this mail only because I   บ
 บ  want to make the life of some leeches better, not because of my hate for  บ
 บ  any one.  We all know that #exceed is HUGE.  25 lines of users is         บ
 บ  concidered normal there.  Every time I join #exceed, I leave every other  บ
 บ  channel I am on, only because I can't keep up and talk with anyone.  The  บ
 บ  flow of information is endless.  Besides, you really can't get any file   บ
 บ  within 5-10 minutes.  All the slots and queues are full.  So I ask        บ
 บ  myself : Why join #exceed, and not join the "small" #groupfiles?  There,  บ
 บ  of course, you won't find 10-12 couriers offering, but you will find 1-2  บ
 บ  with open slots.  When I say the "flow of information" I don't mean only  บ
 บ  the XDCC lists.  I mean the 40-50 joins and /quit's per minute.  It's a   บ
 บ  living hell when you are lagged.  A way to skip this, is to hang around   บ
 บ  #warez_etc.  There, etc-bit "rip's" ONLY the offers from #exceed ;-) and  บ
 บ  displays them publically to the channel.  One last thing, don't flame     บ
 บ  the leeches.  Think about it, if there were no leeches, there wouldn't    บ
 บ  really be a warez scene.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Undi                      บ

 บ  just ..."  EXCUSE ME?  You seem to think that you're better than these    บ
 บ  people?  The fact that you recently retired is not one to give you the    บ

 บ  right to release warez and not label them by the language they are in,    บ
 บ  assuming it is one other than English.  English is the predominant        บ
 บ  language and it could easily be said that it is the national language of  บ
 บ  the Internet.  Thus, it is not necessary to label English programs as     บ
 บ  such.  This is a lot like the Windows 95 craze.  Windows 95 came out and  บ
 บ  all groups that were releasing anything for Windows 3.1 would label it    บ
 บ  as a '95 program because sure, it would work under '95, and many          บ
 บ  couldn't tell the difference.                                             บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Ahh... there's nothing like going to bed at 3:30 am just to get up    บ
 บ  for school at 6:45 am.  Your mother is kicking your bed and shouting at   บ
 บ  the top of her voice and talking about you and that Computer becoming an  บ
 บ  addiction, and why don't you get more sleep? My, how do you ever hope to  บ
 บ  pass high school?  This was a daily routine for me, and I'm sure that a   บ
 บ  lot of the readers are having unpleasant memories of that junk during     บ
 บ  the school year.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The truth is that most traders don't get alot of sleep.  Our grades   บ
 บ  drop in school since we can't think straight, and after a few months of   บ
 บ  having 3-5 hours of sleep a night we become zombies with fucked up        บ
 บ  sleeping schedules and we tend to become a bit irritable.  I have had     บ
 บ  days after a long night on the Net where I was ready to kick any one's    บ
 บ  ass who even dared to talk to me, my nerves were so fried at some         บ
 บ  points.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I know that a lot of us go through this crap due to not getting much  บ
 บ  sleep.  I guess traders won't get much sleep during the summer either     บ
 บ  but there are some serious health concerns that come with not sleeping.   บ
 บ  First, all really good traders put on about 10 pounds due to not having   บ
 บ  the energy/time to go out and exercise.  I used to be a wrestler for my   บ
 บ  old school.  Now I'd have to cut 25 lbs. to even be in shape for it.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Not getting enough rest will gradually weaken your body's resistance  บ
 บ  to colds and flus and fun stuff like that.  And having the sleeping       บ
 บ  schedule of a zombie will begin to make you a very irritable person who   บ
 บ  tends to get into fights or at least be moody at school.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have found that I can stay on top of whatever's going on and get    บ
 บ  all the late days releases if I go to bed at about 4 PM and wake up at    บ
 บ  about midnight.  That gives me about 6 hours to get my trading and        บ
 บ  homework out of the way.  Most traders get burned out after a month or    บ
 บ  two of heavy sleep deprivation and take a week or two off every 2-3       บ
 บ  months just to let their body/mind recouperate.  Traders have a terrible  บ
 บ  diet, get little exercise, and a big lack of sleep.  Golly, we are a      บ
 บ  text book case of a high risk group, hehehe.  Keep that in mind next      บ
 บ  time you get a nasty cold even when it's not cold season.  Most traders   บ
 บ  should take about 1 week out of every 6 weeks off from the scene to rest  บ
 บ  and just relax and let the pressure of the scene roll off a bit before    บ
 บ  jumping back into the fray.  Just my observations, and free advice is     บ
 บ  worth exactly what you pay for it, but just think about it.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Defender Zeta             บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      First off, I would like to say that I really like your e-mag.  The    บ

 บ  business.  Everyone always says that being a courier doesn't take any     บ
 บ  talent, anyone can do it, etc.  And they are right, it doesn't take much  บ
 บ  talent to be a courier.  But it does take a lot of patience.  Now I'm     บ
 บ  not an official courier for any group or anything, but I do offer all     บ
 บ  kinds of shit on IRC.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I try to offer a few megs of stuff every day, but it didn't used to   บ
 บ  be that way.  I used to offer 150 megs of stuff every day, but even       บ
 บ  before that, I ran 3 DCC bots. I quit running the DCC bots when I         บ
 บ  started running a stockbot.  You folks here at RCN Interviewed Dr.        บ
 บ  Jekyll a few issies ago.  A lot of the time, its slots would fill up,     บ
 บ  and people would start messaging me to manually send shit to them.  At    บ
 บ  first, it wasn't too bad, 1 or 2 every 10 minutes or so, but eventually   บ
 บ  it got to where at least 3 lines of my screen were manual send requests,  บ
 บ  so I setup a dcc bot that offered the 5 most popular files on my          บ
 บ  stockbot.  Now, after a few weeks, I ended up with 150 megs of stuff on   บ
 บ  my shell, and my ISP found it.  I didn't get busted or anything, in       บ
 บ  fact, some of my Sysadmins are into warez, but they found the 150 megs    บ
 บ  too much, so they deleted it all, and now I have a quota.  That means     บ
 บ  that now, it's not very easy to offer stuff, but I manage to do it        บ
 บ  still.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I haven't even gotten to the thing I hate most. Though all, oh, I     บ
 บ  don't know, 5 bots and offering myself, people have always bitched at me  บ
 บ  because my queue gets fucked up, my sends are too slow, etc.  This kind   บ
 บ  of shit pisses me off.  My queue gets fucked up because people get        บ
 บ  queued up for shit and then log off, my sends are slow because I have 20  บ
 บ  some odd DCCs going, either that or they are using mIRC and that's        บ
 บ  actually their normal speed.  My DCCs don't connect because too many      บ
 บ  DCCs lag me and my client closes the sends because it thinks they are     บ
 บ  idle sends.  People, the only ones who should bitch about these things    บ
 บ  are the people like me, the people who offer all the time.  I do have     บ
 บ  one last thing to bitch about.  I was a pretty good friend of Dr. Jekyll  บ

 บ  sickening that almost everyone could think only about Stockade.  Fuck,    บ
 บ  that was the last thing I thought about, I felt bad for Dr. Jekyll.  He   บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Just wanted to drop a line about a few things in RCN #18.  First      บ
 บ  off, I am an "old" trader.  I knew of Eagelsoft and The Alliance and was  บ
 บ  even a member of VisionSoft during the C64 era.  But I was busted at the  บ
 บ  age of 15 for carding and did not get another computer until recently,    บ
 บ  September of 1995.  I would like to say that the Internet is a much       บ
 บ  greater medium for trading than BBSs will ever be.  I personally have an  บ
 บ  ISDN line in my house, and it doesn't help one bit for BBS couriering.    บ
 บ  Why would I bother when I can get 128kbs on the net?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      But in a way, the Internet also drags the scene down.  You have to    บ
 บ  deal much more with assholes than I ever did in my BBS days.  You also    บ
 บ  don't have a coolng off period, egos clash and there's no time to think   บ
 บ  through your actions.  One guy gets pissed over one shitty release and    บ
 บ  NARCS?!?!?!!  This is absolutely disgusting!  Back in my days on BBSs     บ
 บ  you posted a mean letter, cooled off, and went on to something else.      บ
 บ  Here it's bankick this, delete user that, deop him, ban her, you get the  บ
 บ  point.  But I didn't write this just to bitch about certain members of    บ
 บ  the scene.  I personally have not had the pleasure of coming in contact   บ
 บ  with the most "elite" members of the scene because I hang out on the      บ
 บ  Undernet, which is fine for me, mostly because my group, Eclipse, is the  บ
 บ  best on there, and yet we do not compete with THC, Empire, RiSC or any    บ
 บ  of the larger courier groups.  Although I do know THC is now a release    บ
 บ  group ;-).  We hang on the undernet, deal with 1 or 2 splits a day, and   บ
 บ  that's it.  Not too much bullshit goes on there.  So why is it that       บ
 บ  every time I try to improve Eclipse by getting in contact with release    บ
 บ  groups, other courier groups, etc., that everyone feels it necessary to   บ
 บ  tell me to move to EFNet?  I don't care if I ever am a *GOD* first of     บ
 บ  all, and second I can spread my name and warez to 3000+ people who don't  บ
 บ  have attitude problems because they hang out in #exceed and leech and     บ
 บ  think that makes them elite.  Why is the Undernet bashed so often?  I'm   บ
 บ  sorry I don't understand, but it makes no sense.  A release group can     บ
 บ  get their releases to 3000+ people unrestricted through us, but would     บ
 บ  rather fight and bicker with 20+ other groups who hang ou on EFNet        บ
 บ  because it's cool.  Well 300 splits a day ain't cool with me, I like to   บ
 บ  finish conversations I start =).                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Dupe                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hi, this is Netman (Original, huh?) and I'm currently at what you     บ
 บ  would consider the very bottom of the scene hierarchy.  I'm not to any    บ
 บ  degree unhappy with this situation either.  I'm perfectly content with    บ
 บ  getting my warez the old-fashioned way -- through local boards, and on a  บ
 บ  rare occasion, from AOL.  I get my 28.8 I-Net service through GNN, and    บ
 บ  therefore cannot join any of the K-R4D IRC channels.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Having joined the scene late in '96, I happened to catch a few        บ
 บ  months of what some consider the good old pre-Net days.  You remember --  บ
 บ  when game releases were under 10 disks, and 60+ hours of play, not the    บ
 บ  other way around.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I think that the scene today has gotten too impersonnal.  With the    บ
 บ  net couriers, the files can be sent out world-wide without ever           บ
 บ  downloading them.  Yes, I can see how that can bring warez to local       บ
 บ  boards faster, but personally, I liked it much better when you could      บ
 บ  send a message to the uploader asking him how he got the damn thing to    บ
 บ  work if you're having problems.  Nowadays, the release will be spread     บ
 บ  all over the world before somebody downloads it and realizes that it      บ
 บ  doesn't work.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Although I recognize that I would not be able to call up a local      บ
 บ  number and get all the latest releases if it weren't for these couriers,  บ
 บ  I have to wonder as to their motivation.  I mean it used to be that you   บ
 บ  spent about three hours a day uploading, so that the next day, you could  บ
 บ  spend six hours leeching something.  Anything that you downloaded, you    บ
 บ  got for your personal use, and only later cared about uploading it        บ
 บ  somewhere else.  Thus you unarchived the program and tested it on your    บ
 บ  machine, and your conscience wouldn't allow you to spread it further if   บ
 บ  it didn't work.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Today, people spend much of their lives, just transfering stuff over  บ
 บ  the net, not caring whether what they spread is some pitiful piece of     บ
 บ  crap or not.  I personally do not understand that.  Why would somebody    บ
 บ  try to do all that, waste their lives spreading stuff around, and not     บ
 บ  even bothering to see what it is.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Because of that, I rarely download even the most anticipated of       บ
 บ  releases if the releasing group is one unknown to me.  And if I do        บ
 บ  download it, it's only after a thorough examination of the NFOs inside.   บ
 บ  Another thing that I dislike is the way the groups double, and sometimes  บ
 บ  triple pack their releases.  Not only does it leave more junk rotting     บ
 บ  around on your hard drive, but it also often makes it impossible to scan  บ
 บ  all your archives for viruses.  I for example have gotten about 3         บ
 บ  infections during the last week alone.  All this said, I have to          บ
 บ  recognize the value that the net scene has to us average "joe-shmoes."    บ
 บ  In the time I have come to the scene, you had to call around a number of  บ
 บ  boards before you could find what you need, but now you can get any file  บ
 บ  off of any local board with no hassle.  Also the development of the       บ
 บ  CD-ROMs and the CD-ROM writing devices has meant the ability to actually  บ
 บ  store offline files offline.  Now you can request any old file (and I     บ
 บ  think many would agree that the best releases gamewise were done in the   บ
 บ  1992-1994 period) and the sysop can get it for you if it's stored         บ
 บ  offline.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I guess that while there are still people like me, who don't have  บ
 บ  ISDN connections, or unlimited Internet access, and who like a good game  บ
 บ  rather than an interactive movie any day of the week, there will still    บ
 บ  be a use for the local scene, with its "oh-so-lame" 5 and under node      บ
 บ  boards, and traditional traders.  And the net scene will be viewed by     บ
 บ  some as something remote, faceless, and unreachable.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Netman                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You know, it's entertaining for me to read your zine.  I sit here     บ
 บ  looking at the at the monitor, and listen to the kick ass music, and 50%  บ
 บ  of what I see is either someone bitching at a group, or someone bitching  บ
 บ  at RCN for publishing someone else's bitching at a group.  I don't get    บ
 บ  that.  These people feel so insecure in their position in the scene that  บ
 บ  they must put down others to hold their position?  That's bull            บ
 บ  shit.%12Dear RCN,The most elite people in the scene are not the ones      บ
 บ  that sit, oped on some halfway decent channel, ignoring everyone except   บ
 บ  their co-ops.  The most elite are the people that can get along with      บ
 บ  other people, no matter who the fuck they are, or where they stand in     บ
 บ  the scene's rating system.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The most elite are the people that have enough patience, know enough  บ
 บ  about life, and have enough self-esteem to just take someone else's       บ
 บ  attack on them and just get overit.  Think about it, if you read the      บ
 บ  bitches everyone has in the last few releases of RCN, you might realize   บ
 บ  that about 90% of these bitchings can be eliminated by taking out the     บ
 บ  scene's way of classifying people.  Sure, some people get on IRC, and     บ
 บ  are total fuckers, and just screw any chance they have about getting      บ
 บ  someplace where they will make a difference, but, is that a reason to     บ
 บ  label them as lame?  Or to ignore their questions that they ask you?      บ
 บ  Hell no.  You should look at it like this, these people obviously look    บ
 บ  up to you, in some sense, because most people would not ask a total       บ
 บ  dumbass how to do the kind of things these people are asking.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyway, this is getting a little long, so here is what I am trying    บ
 บ  to say.  You head people in fATE, or MadCrew, or any other respectable    บ
 บ  group, were you EVER in the same position that these other people are     บ
 บ  in?  If you say "no," then you obviously are lucker than most people      บ
 บ  that try to get in the scene.  Almost everybody starts out as an          บ
 บ  annoying little punk that doesn't know what the fuck a ping is.  So, why  บ
 บ  not just give a little of your knowledge to who you used to be?  There    บ
 บ  is no need to label a person 'lame' just because he is just starting      บ
 บ  out.  Hell, someday the person that asks you how to ping someone, will    บ
 บ  likely be the person that heads the group you are in, or a group          บ
 บ  competing with yours.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There should be no enemies here, after all, the #1 thing that brings  บ
 บ  down groups is their conflicts with other groups, or conflicts within     บ
 บ  the group itself.  Just fucking get over it, someone bitches you out,     บ
 บ  fine.  You don't need to bitch them out back.  It should not work that    บ
 บ  way.  If someone bitches you out, just write back, with the facts, in a   บ
 บ  NON-ATTACKING way.  If you attack someone, they will probably attack you  บ
 บ  back.  Just fucking don't listen to them.  I mean, the scene in a whole   บ
 บ  would be SO FUCKING MUCH better if all groups got along, or at least      บ
 บ  tried to get along.  You couriers and releasers have tasks that you are   บ
 บ  supposed to do to get shit out, distribute it, and then go get more       บ
 บ  shit.  You expected that responsibility, but where does it say you have   บ
 บ  to compete with others with the same job?  Nowhere.  Well, competition    บ
 บ  is not the problem.  It is just all the hatred groups have for each       บ
 บ  other.  All the unneeded hatred.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Quinto                    บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : <Undisclosed>             Interviewee : Jay Wilbur           บ
 บ    Subject  : iD Software on Piracy     Affiliation : iD Representative    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : First off, just last night, at approximately 2 am, tKLP packaged    บ
 บ        and released the fully registered version of Quake to the mass      บ
 บ        public, is iD software aware of that?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  JAY : You are the second person to tell me this.  tKLP has denied it to   บ
 บ        me in email claiming to know the real bad guy that released Quake.  บ
 บ        He said he would give me the information on the Quake supplier if   บ
 บ        I paid him a reward.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What was your response to tKLP, do you believe him?  tKLP           บ
 บ        definitely did package the software, but he might not be willing    บ
 บ        to turn in his Quake supplier for a quick reward.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  JAY : As a rule I never believe anyone who does not have the balls to     บ
 บ        use his own name.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are the effects of having tKLP releasing a fully registered    บ
 บ        version of iD Software's major release Quake, even before it has    บ
 บ        hit the stores?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  JAY : If the release is contained to the Internet, then it should only    บ
 บ        be a pain in the ass for us.  If the release should make it to      บ
 บ        retail.  We will be forced to bring every possible legal remedy to  บ
 บ        bear on the bad guys to protect our copyrighted work.  We are       บ
 บ        talking federal crime here.  Were you around when DOOM II was       บ
 บ        released?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : No, but could you please describe the event?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  JAY : Similar situation to this, a beta version hit the net and it        บ
 บ        turned out to be a major pain in the ass.  The bad guys got         บ
 บ        fucking reamed, and don't ask about it, I will be inclined not to   บ
 บ        answer.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Who got reamed and how, unless you do describe the consequences of  บ
 บ        the matter, people will dismiss it as a petty remark.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  JAY : Fuck them, they will know when they get reamed.  Violations of      บ
 บ        Federal copyright laws are very serious crimes.  I believe the      บ
 บ        penalties are covered in texts maintained on government WWW sites.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since the people who released Doom II was "reamed" and thus, payed  บ
 บ        for their crimes, and iD Software does suspect that tKLP was the    บ
 บ        one who released Quake, will iD sotware ream tKLP (assuming there   บ
 บ        is ample evidence to prosecute)?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  JAY : If, as result, bad guys do pirate Quake and ship it to retail, we   บ
 บ        WILL go after the bad guys.  There was a CD factory in Germany      บ
 บ        churning out pirate CDs of DOOM II for retail.  We went overseas,   บ
 บ        and kicked their asses.  We ended up shutting that company down     บ
 บ        and tossing the principals into jail.  We are very nice guys, but   บ
 บ        we will not stand by and be ripped off.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is iD Software aware that the fully registered version of Quake is  บ
 บ        being distributed at this very moment on ftp.cdrom.com in           บ
 บ        directory /pub/idgames/quake/incoming/quakeb3.zip?                  บ

 บ        administrator takes it out when he becomes aware of it, but then    บ
 บ        some other loser puts it back up in /incoming, etc.                 บ

 บ        Quake piracy incident to the full extent of the law?  I'm aware     บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Erupt                บ
 บ    Subject  : The Problem with GODS     Affiliation : ex-GODS Senior       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You recently quit GODS (Guild of Distributors) even though you      บ
 บ        were a senior of that group, and GODS was rumored to be one of the  บ
 บ        new courier groups that could rival and possibly out courier RiSC   บ
 บ        (Rise in Superior Couriering).  Why did you quit GODS?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EPT : Many things led to my departure since the group had started.  I     บ
 บ        was very mad about how things had been setup and who was awarded    บ
 บ        certain positions in the group even though they had not done any    บ
 บ        work to deserve it.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Was that the only reason why you decided to leave GODS?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EPT : No, this this was but one of the many problems the group was        บ
 บ        having.  GODS was also plagued with many problems because many of   บ
 บ        the other seniors were not doing anything for the group.  They      บ
 บ        were just sitting on their asses whining.  This fustrated me at     บ
 บ        times since Gahn, Silent Mobius, and I worked very hard in our      บ
 บ        positions to make the group prosper.  We did not selfishly worry    บ
 บ        so much about ourselves like everyone else in the group.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I assume then, that all these problems just came piling over on     บ
 บ        you.  What finally tipped you over the edge and made you decide to  บ
 บ        quit GODS?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EPT : I finnaly tipped over the edge on Sunday, June 16, when I got into  บ
 บ        an argument with Quazimodem.  I had never seen Quazimodem do        บ
 บ        ANYTHING for the group.  He was supposed to be the original         บ
 บ        founder of the group, but he didn't even hang in the channel much.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did the argument start?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EPT : Gahn and I were just sitting in the channel and out of no where,    บ
 บ        Quazimodem comes out and says, "Gahn, why are you such an           บ
 บ        asshole?"  Just seeing Quazimodem disrespect a hardworking          บ
 บ        coordinator of GODS like that really steamed me, and then I saw     บ
 บ        him kick Gahn out of the channel.  I was so mad at this point!  I   บ
 บ        decided to defend Gahn who is a very good friend of mine, and a     บ
 บ        damn hard worker for GODS.  Quazimodem responded to me with the     บ
 บ        comment, "I don't give a fuck who you are!"  That just blew me      บ
 บ        over the edge so I changed the topic on the channel stating that I  บ
 บ        had left the group, and then I left, and that was the end of it.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you believe that Quazimodem is a bad influence on the group?     บ
 บ        He was one of the original members of GODS 2 years ago, and is a    บ
 บ        big part of why it is back up today, perhaps he felt that you were  บ
 บ        not giving him the respect he felt he deserved?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        to courier, courier your _OWN_ warez.  Not those of other groups    บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Faraway              บ
 บ    Subject  : SNES Emulators WORK???    Affiliation : SPW Translator       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I've seen SNES emulators for years now released here and there,     บ
 บ        and I've downloaded nearly every single one of them, but NONE of    บ
 บ        them were even close to what you could call a working SNES          บ
 บ        emulator.  I've talked to many people about SNES emulators and      บ
 บ        they too vouch that all of the SNES emulators released in the past  บ
 บ        few years are bogus fakes that don't work.  Has that changed in     บ
 บ        the past year?  Are SNES emulators still fakes put out by really    บ
 บ        lame people?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : Ok.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Could you go into a little more detail?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : Yes, it's true, I've gotten a whole mess of SNES emulators that     บ
 บ        were FAKE, but things changed this past year.  First discovered by  บ
 บ        Pan of Anthrox was a SNES emulator from Japan called SPW (Super     บ
 บ        Paso Windows).  At first, I thought that it might yet be another    บ
 บ        fake, but after I tested it, I found out it wasn't a fake.  The     บ
 บ        working SNES emulator changed channel #SNES, the ops of that        บ
 บ        channel used to say "There is no such thing as an SNES EMULATOR,"   บ
 บ        but they stopped saying that and instead, the ops had to start      บ
 บ        telling people to stop mentioning it so much.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is that when you started channel #SNESEmu?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : Yes, two of my friends and I started #SNESEMU, so people could ask  บ
 บ        about it freely.  The SNES scene has totally changed since the      บ
 บ        advent of SNES emulators.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : But aren't the only working SNES emulators Japanese, created by     บ
 บ        Japanese programmers?  Can you BUY these SNES emulators?  Does a    บ
 บ        company officially make them, or is it an underground operation?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : The Brain, who speaks English, decided to start giving the writer   บ
 บ        of SPW some competition.  Yes, SPW was made by a Japanese           บ
 บ        programmer, and yes, sadly he does have a registration fee, but     บ
 บ        with so many crackers these days, you don't really have to pay 60   บ
 บ        dollars to register it.  I have information tha the SPW is made by  บ
 บ        one person, and not by a company.  I don't think that SNES          บ
 บ        emulators need to be spread underground, there is nothing really    บ
 บ        illegal about emulating another system as long as you don't pirate  บ
 บ        and distribute the games for that system.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Right.  I am aware that there's now an English version of SPW,      บ
 บ        what part do you play in the translation of the Japanese SPW to     บ
 บ        the English SPW which now allows most people to download and enjoy  บ
 บ        SNES games?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : Well to tell you the truth, my two friends and I were the first to  บ
 บ        translate SPW, it.  It wasn't a full translation.  We had no idea   บ
 บ        if our guesses were right, but later on, when other people started  บ
 บ        translating too, we saw how right we really were.  I was the one    บ
 บ        translating.  Kaboom and Nic Zak were just guessing and playing     บ
 บ        around with the buttons.  Resource Workshop is great for            บ
 บ        translating.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many people still claim that the whole SPW business is fake and     บ
 บ        does not work.  I've personally downloaded SPW to test it myself,   บ
 บ        and it has not worked as advertised.  I've 16 megs of RAM on my     บ
 บ        100 MHz Pentium, why has SPW failed to work?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : SPW doesn't work on everyone's computer, and some people think      บ
 บ        that the SPW, and SNES emulator scene is fake, but to tell you the  บ
 บ        truth, it's not.  I have a 90 MHz Pentium, running Windows 95 with  บ
 บ        16 megs of RAM, and I've been able to play games like Killer        บ
 บ        Instict.  It seems that SPW chooses which computers it wants to     บ
 บ        run on, I would suggest, that you people who don't have WinG        บ
 บ        installed should install it, because it is required in order for    บ
 บ        SPW to work.  I don't know any other reasons for it not working.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned earlier that working SNES emulators have changed the  บ
 บ        scene, how is that so?  As far as I can tell, most people still     บ
 บ        consider SNES emulators to be a waste of time.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : It has changed the scene, for example, let's say you're a coder     บ
 บ        for the 65816 CPU (the SNES), you don't have to send your program   บ
 บ        to the SNES any more, and waste time.  All you need to do is use    บ
 บ        Windows, and write your program in a notepad, assemble it, and run  บ
 บ        it on the emulator.  The emulator saves a lot of time copying       บ
 บ        games to disks and putting them in your console.  Loading up a 3    บ
 บ        disk SNES console game would take me around 10 minutes if I used    บ
 บ        the console and not the SNES eumator.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where can one a version of SPW?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : One can find SPW being offered in #SNESEmu and can also be found    บ
 บ        on http://home.pacific.net.sg/~bkchaw/ and                          บ
 บ        http://iceonline.com:/home/thebrain/vsmc/.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has Nintendo Corporation showed any resentment toward seeing that   บ
 บ        SNES emulators are now widely available for pirates?  People used   บ
 บ        to have to buy consoles which would cost anywhere from 300 to 500   บ
 บ        dollars in order to play pirated SNES games, but now, all people    บ
 บ        have to do is download a 600kb emulator.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SPW : No, as far as I know, Nintendo hasn't even said one word about      บ
 บ        this, no one has been contacted or anything, it looks to me like    บ
 บ        Nintendo can't do anything about it.  Like I said earlier, it's     บ
 บ        not really illegal to emulate the SNES on a PC.  The only thing     บ
 บ        Nintendo would really be pissed at is that there are a lot of       บ
 บ        people that offer SNES games for downloading.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Dupe                 บ
 บ    Subject  : Eclipse                   Affiliation : Eclipse President    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I have not seen much of it on effnet, but I'm aware that it's       บ
 บ        presence is growing as one of the premiere undernet groups.  What   บ
 บ        kind of group courier group is Eclipse?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : Eclipse was started by Funky Boy and a couple of other members      บ
 บ        that were in Intel, including me.  When Intel disbanded, we wanted  บ
 บ        to start a channel for trading among friends, but as interest       บ
 บ        grew, we decided to take it further than that and make it a         บ
 บ        full-blown courier group.  We are well known on the undernet, but   บ
 บ        we are just starting to leak over onto effnet.  Funky Boy stepped   บ
 บ        down due to lack of time, and now its my job to get us connected.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why didn't you start Eclipse on effnet right from the start?        บ
 บ        There are a lot more people who are on effnet than undernet, and    บ
 บ        thus, it's much more widely recognized and would benefit your       บ
 บ        group much more.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : Eclipse was never going to be a group, so we chose the undernet     บ
 บ        because their is less lag, splits, and a lot less people.  We       บ
 บ        didn't want to be constantly bothered.  The attitudes of the        บ
 บ        people on undernet are much better, we don't have 500 losers        บ
 บ        hanging out in #Exceed leeching and calling themselves elite.       บ
 บ        Most people there are doing it for fun, and that is what we stand   บ
 บ        for.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : If one wants to join Eclipse, how would one get connected to        บ
 บ        undernet?  Is there a channel #Eclipse on undernet?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : Yes, there was even one on effnet for awhile, but the undernet is   บ
 บ        our home base.  Just join the undernet, and then join #Eclipse ,    บ
 บ        its not even +i, so we get a lot of visitors.  We have an           บ
 บ        application generator to make it easy for those interested.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does one join the undernet?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : There are tons of servers, but the best is                          บ
 บ        atlanta.ga.us.undernet.org.  It is the newest server and always     บ
 บ        seems to be the fastest.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many members make up Eclipse?  Is Eclipse large in numbers?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : We currently have 13 dedicated members, and a few trial members,    บ
 บ        but we have tried to keep the numbers down, to insure we get        บ
 บ        quality members.  We could have a lot more, but we don't need them  บ
 บ        to be efficient.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange) couriers by offering a lot of     บ
 บ        people who idle in #Exceed, RiSC (Rise in Superior Couriering)      บ
 บ        couriers by being the fastest on FTP sites, and Everlast couriers   บ
 บ        by being the fastest on bulletin boards.  Eclipse does not have an  บ
 บ        offer channel like fATE, and Eclipse does not have FTP sites like   บ
 บ        RiSC, and I doubt Eclipse has board couriers like Everlast!  How    บ
 บ        does Eclipse courier?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : We don't pretend to be the biggest, but we do have a lot of         บ
 บ        members dedicated to spreading warez.  We move a lot of warez each  บ
 บ        day, and we don't try to rate ourselves.  If we get everything      บ
 บ        out, we've done our job.  Not to mention, I can think of numerous   บ
 บ        occasions when I have downloaded bad software from fATE and RiSC.   บ
 บ        We check ALL warez before we put our name on it.  We currently      บ
 บ        have 6 offer bots, and 4 dedicated t-1 sites, not to mention a      บ
 บ        slew of independent sites we supply.  As far as I'm concerned, we   บ
 บ        do an excellent job, especially for a group that is only 4 months   บ
 บ        old.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you mean by, "We check ALL warez before we put our name on  บ
 บ        it?"                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : You won't be seeing Eclipse upload fake warez or bad cracks.  We    บ
 บ        try to actually RUN the programs before we courier them.  If we     บ
 บ        find out we uploaded a bad disk somewhere, it becomes our first     บ
 บ        priority to fix that, so that the people on the sites don't waste   บ
 บ        time downloading it.  We care a lot about the people we courier to  บ
 บ        and would not want to see them download fake warez.  We know what   บ
 บ        we are and we don't need other groups to tell us.  As long as our   บ
 บ        siteops stay happy with Eclipse, we will earn the recognition we    บ
 บ        deserve.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : That's a great attitude and I just wish more courier groups         บ
 บ        thought like that.   Anyway, are you aware that there's also a      บ
 บ        games group called Eclipse?  They haven't released in over 3        บ
 บ        months, but that's because it specializes in floppy games, and      บ
 บ        there haven't been too many floppy games released by companies in   บ
 บ        the past months.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : No, I was not aware of that, I have heard rumors that there was     บ
 บ        another group called Eclipse, but I didn't pay much attention.  We  บ
 บ        are Eclipse Couriers, so if people get us confused, I can't do      บ
 บ        much about it.  All I can do is try to keep the name Eclipse in a   บ
 บ        good light, and if that group benefits from it, I'm happy for       บ
 บ        them.  Although this could get ugly if the games group Eclipse is   บ
 บ        lame and it keeps us down, but that's just another hurdle to jump   บ
 บ        if it does come.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are your future plans for Eclipse?  It's only a courier group  บ
 บ        right now, but perhaps you might want to venture into releasing as  บ
 บ        well?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ECP : Well, that would be nice, but right now we are focusing on being    บ
 บ        couriers, we do however need a quality release group to courier     บ
 บ        for.  And we WILL be picky, I know we don't have the experience of  บ
 บ        other courier groups, but we will not compromise quality and        บ
 บ        courier for "fly-by night release groups".  We only want to move    บ
 บ        GOOD cracks and GOOD warez.  If you spend all your time making      บ
 บ        patches for your releases, don't bother talking to me.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Reporter : Nevesis                   Interviewee : Nightsky             บ
 บ    Subject  : AOD Survived?             Affiliation : AOD President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Am I correct in saying that Morbid left the scene due to personal   บ
 บ        reasons?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : Yes, or else he would have never left.  He loved, the scene.  We    บ
 บ        all know how addictive the scene can be.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yes, that we do.  Well Morbid was a great guy, we can only hope to  บ
 บ        see him back soon.  Could you please tell me how big AOD (Angels    บ
 บ        of Death) has gotten and how long it has been around for?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : AOD was founded by Morbid and I in early 1996 and was started from  บ
 บ        scratch.  We didn't know much about the scene at the time, but we   บ
 บ        grew into it and got some good couriers and sites.  I think most    บ
 บ        people would now be surprised at the speed of the AOD sites.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some of the goals for AOD that you think will place it in  บ
 บ        a good position heading into the future of this doggy dog scene?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : We need to get ourselves established as a respected group and we    บ
 บ        need to move up in the sites scene, and try to get our best         บ
 บ        couriers on the big sites of our competition.  But above all, we    บ
 บ        want to have some fun.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Has AOD had any major problems with other groups putting it down?   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : Not really, but we often get underestimated.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Recently there was some mish mash going on about the group called   บ
 บ        Nemesis, and they tried to get a few groups to merge with them.     บ
 บ        Is it true that AOD was close to merging or even did merge for a    บ
 บ        short period of time with this mysterious group?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : Well this supposed merger happened when I was away (5 am in the     บ
 บ        morning) so I didn't know there was something going on.  The next   บ
 บ        day I had to put things back together and undo the things that had  บ
 บ        happened.  Apparently, someone thought it was a good idea to form   บ
 บ        a group out of all the small groups around (which I would count     บ
 บ        AOD as part of).  The next day I got everything back together and   บ
 บ        introduced a new co-president and we are kicking ass as we did      บ
 บ        before.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you're telling me that when the President was away, some of      บ
 บ        your members decided to merge themselves without your               บ
 บ        jurisdiction?  That isn't a very good thing!  Who was the one that  บ
 บ        got appointed as the new co-president?  Does he have any            บ
 บ        experience running a group?  If so, which group?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : There was quite a lot of chaos and in chaos, things happen.         บ
 บ        Apparently most members thought I would agree to merge, but I       บ
 บ        never did.  The next day, I made it clear that I would never agree  บ
 บ        to a merge and all my group members were pleased with that          บ
 บ        response.  As for the new co-president, I introduced Acid Flux to   บ
 บ        the group.  He hasn't gotten any experience but it doesn't take     บ
 บ        much to run a group.  Obviously, I succeeded!  He is a cool guy     บ
 บ        and I am sure he will do a good job.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I hope you were right in that decision.  On a lighter note, are     บ
 บ        there any openings in AOD that you would like to make public?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  AOD : Well, great Internet couriers are always welcome and a BBS courier  บ
 บ        coordinator would be nice right about now.  If you're interested    บ
 บ        in applying to AOD please join #AOD on the Effnet.  I would just    บ
 บ        like to say that I miss Morbid on the Internet although he is       บ
 บ        still a good friend that lives just a block away from me!           บ
