                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/06/96 -> 06/12/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/13/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/23/96 -> 05/29/96            ณ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/30/96 -> 06/05/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Spacebucks *100% Working*   [xx/35]                                       บ
 บ                                         บ
 บ  |Also works on Windows 3.1 & 3.11 |                                       บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thanks to M8 for releasing this previously non-working game.   In     บ
 บ  it, you race against other racers in an effort to make your planet just   บ
 บ  a lot cooler and better than the others.  Basically a sim game, but with  บ
 บ  planets.  Plenty of shit to do in it, building all kinds of things.       บ
 บ  Graphics are ok, but the words are sometimes a little to dark to read.    บ
 บ  Pretty good music and sfx.  Only bother to get it if you really think     บ
 บ  you'll sit down and play it for long periods of time.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 62/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  |___|\__\   \________  /___\__\__   \______\             PHANTOM WIZARD   บ
 บ  +--------\___/๗e๗/aL!\/--------/_____\-----+                              บ
 บ     S.T.O.R.M (c) American Softworks 31/31                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, as Ionizer stated, this thing doesn't work at all from MS-DOS.  บ
 บ  It keeps asking for the CD. But if run under Win95 in MSDOS mode, it      บ
 บ  runs just fine.  I also got it to work in Win95 mode, but it ran much     บ
 บ  slower and crashed when loading the main game, so.. Anywayz, after the    บ
 บ  game was up and running, it played ok on my 486/66 with all the options   บ
 บ  turned on (Parallax and High Details), so it probably jams on a p75+.     บ
 บ  You play some sub type machine and you have different missions with each  บ
 บ  level.  You collect different weapons and there are plenty of obstacles   บ
 บ  and enemies.  It's pretty much just a straight arcade shooter with an     บ
 บ  underwater background.  Nice SVGA grafix and they managed to leave in     บ
 บ  some sfx and music which are ok too. I enjoyed playing this game for      บ
 บ  about 2 hours, which I then got bored and frustrated with it. Not worth   บ
 บ  the 100+ megs of HD it takes. They should rip out all the Win95 and       บ
 บ  nonworking shit and then re-release a smaller ver.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 60/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ      Napalm goes and breaks the 40 disk limit that they originally agreed  บ
 บ  to set.  However it doesn't seem to matter much since the game didn't     บ
 บ  work for me anyway, although some others said they have gotten it to      บ
 บ  work, others have had a million different problems with it.  I followed   บ
 บ  the nfo exactly, ran the install, installed to where it asked to, and     บ
 บ  ran lb.exe.  All it did was sit there, no errors, no nothing, just        บ
 บ  lockup.  I noticed that the installer made two subdirs of "longbow" so I  บ
 บ  even arj'ed it w/ one dir, but still nothing.  Nothing is corrupt, so     บ
 บ  I'd love to hear what I did wrong.  Apparently there is a new type of     บ
 บ  .exe that has a mind of it's own and only works when it feels like it     บ
 บ  for only certain people.                                                  บ

 บ  ======= \___/ === \___/ === \__/ ==                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's been a while since I made fun of one of these kiddie games.      บ
 บ  This one is supposed to teach kids about "the information superhighway"   บ
 บ  and more about computers.  I sincerely question the way they teach kids.  บ
 บ  The game has this singing dog, Gus, and he sings all these stupid songs   บ
 บ  with words that barely rhyme.  Everything is called like                  บ
 บ  cyber-something, like cybertoys, cyberpark.  The thing is, they have      บ
 บ  absolutely nothing to do with computers.  If you go into the laundromat,  บ
 บ  to clean your clothes, there's a little bag with clothing.  You click on  บ
 บ  it, and some alien dork says "a modem is used to send data over a phone   บ
 บ  line".  WTF DOES DIRTY LAUNDRY HAVE TO DO WITH MODEMS?! In fact what the  บ
 บ  fuck does a laundromat have anything to do with computers or the inet.    บ
 บ  The title is extremely misleading, someone wanna call the Better          บ
 บ  Business Bureau?  Anyway, you basically walk around from place to place   บ
 บ  and click on anything on the screen and it will do a shitty little        บ
 บ  animation.  I can't even reccomend you getting this for your little       บ
 บ  brother or sister to help them learn, because it is too retarded.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 34/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ    American CivilWar (c)Interactive Magic x/26                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This war simulation game has a very informative and nicely done       บ
 บ  intro.  The game itself is the usual war type.  You're giving a map type  บ
 บ  playing field.  You have your army's and brigades and whatnot.  You       บ
 บ  manage the supplies and moves and when to attack and when to defend.      บ
 บ  Nothing we haven't seen before.  The usual million of differnet factors   บ
 บ  that effect the outcome are in here, with the thousands of options.       บ
 บ  Looks like a nice, well put together game.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 62/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ   Terry Bradshaw Fantasy Football   [X/2]                                  บ
 บ  +------------------------------------------+                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Here's a simple yet complex (impossible you say?) fantasy league      บ
 บ  program.  It allows you to set up your fantasy league so that you can     บ
 บ  waste all your money on guys who end up being injured.  I'm not too       บ
 บ  familar with fantasy league programs, but this one, I assume, has all     บ
 บ  you need, since it has tons of shit to set up and stuff.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                      RATING : 70/100 <if you need it>                      บ
 บ                        RATING : 5/100 <if you dont>                        บ

 บ  QUAKE v0.91 - Shareware - id Software                                     บ
 บ  Supports multiple players via modem                                       บ
 บ  or network, in coop or deathmatch.                                        บ
 บ  Part x of 7                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well here's the review on all of betas/SW for Quake.  I know many of  บ
 บ  you will get all pissed at me for this review, but to you- Go fuck        บ
 บ  yourself.  Quake, the big deal doom like game, the one that's supposed    บ
 บ  to top all the rest, the one that is supposed to have shit we could       บ
 บ  never dream of.  Would someone like to tell me where all this is?  I      บ
 บ  mean I'm not giving up on it, I know it's a beta/SW, but is this game     บ
 บ  really any different from the shit we've already seen.  The graphics are  บ
 บ  nothing spectacular, and if you are amazed by the sky graphics, then I    บ
 บ  know tons of web sites where you can look at background type shit just    บ
 บ  like that.  The game simply is nothing spectacular, yet.  You're all too  บ
 บ  hyped up about it, with the idea that it will be the best game out ever,  บ
 บ  and it really isn't.  That's not to say it isn't good, it's still good,   บ
 บ  but way over-rated and way over-hyped.  Oh, and spare me the bullshit     บ
 บ  about my computer not being good enough for this, I ran it on my          บ
 บ  sister's p/100, and it didn't change my feelings about the game.  Some    บ
 บ  good things to comment about it:  The nice outlay of the game lets you    บ
 บ  pick the level you want to go through by walking to it, rather than just  บ
 บ  selecting it from a menu.  The nice realism when walking up slopes, that  บ
 บ  makes you fall back down if you stop.  All in all, I think the            บ
 บ  "catacomb" idea for doom like games has been way overdone, which is why   บ
 บ  when DN3D came out, it was a big hit, because it wasn't just those        บ
 บ  boring catacombs.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The game is also very dark, and making it brighter just doesn't seem  บ
 บ  to help out much.  A million of you will prolly complain about this       บ
 บ  review, and I don't mind it, but if you do, all I ask is you prove to me  บ
 บ  what is so great about it, why it's so much better than any other         บ
 บ  game... because I know you'll have a hard time doing it.  You're going    บ
 บ  to need a pretty powerful computer to play this full screen, 640X, and    บ
 บ  not have any slowdown, so go buy a p/100.  I don't want to give the       บ
 บ  impression that this game sucks, it's not that, it just may not live up   บ
 บ  to how good you may have thought it would be.   Oh, and don't bother to   บ
 บ  get it if you have a 486, it's too slow, and the graphics are degraded    บ
 บ  to 320, and it looks real bad in that mode.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyway, as for "what is what" the 8.5 meg is the "SW" beta, only      บ
 บ  containing the first of the four different levels.  The 21 megger is the  บ
 บ  full thing, still called a beta, but it has all of the levels.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  that say it's a beta and it's the same exact size as the 21 megger.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Ionizer> What *DID* you release?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ         the actual final that will be in the stores is we dont have the    บ
 บ         400 megs of music, no modem play , and you cant hack up dead       บ
 บ         bodies.                                                            บ

 บ            beta?                                                           บ

 บ         over the place.                                                    บ

 บ  it, get the ROR version, otherwise just go fetch the 21 meg zip.  Or you  บ
 บ  can always just get the official SW version if you're a faggot.  It       บ
 บ  still gets a good rating, cuz it's still a good game, it's not necessary  บ
 บ  to talk much more about it, you know what it is and what it's got.        บ

 บ      AFTERLIFE (c) LucasArts [01/40]                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Haha, this is a pretty clever and witty sim game.  You are the        บ
 บ  controller of both heaven and hell, and it's your job to make sure the    บ
 บ  dead are either punished or satisfied.  The game had a nice intro, funny  บ
 บ  at times.  Then when it loads up it gives ya some humor, like instead of  บ
 บ  just saying "load ##%" it says "Warming burrioo ##%" and some other       บ
 บ  funny shit.  The game has nice tutorials to help you figure out how to    บ
 บ  play.  Mrs. Heaven and Mr. Hell are your little sidekicks to help you     บ
 บ  figure out what to do.  They have some, at times, witty things to say to  บ
 บ  each other.  The graphics for the game coulda been a little better, but   บ
 บ  they are still good, and the sound is fine.  This is a well put together  บ
 บ  quality game.  If you like sim city, you will defintely want to check     บ
 บ  this one out.  It will hog a nice 150+ megs though.  Oh, and be sure to   บ
 บ  pick up the dos addon if you don't have win95.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 82/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  game by Hybrid, the king of the foot fairies.  This one is very similar   บ

 บ  my keys, but they didn't do anything, and it just seemed like no matter   บ
 บ  what option I picked, the game played itself anyway.  However, I could    บ
 บ  still tell what the game was like. Your average soccer game, nothing      บ
 บ  great.                                                                    บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off  anyone who calls others "lamers" is anything but elite.    บ
 บ  I feel that being elite is possesing a higher level of knowledge than     บ
 บ  the majority of the people that do what you do.  I mean if you are the    บ
 บ  smartest scientist then you are an elite scientist.  Being elite does     บ
 บ  not mean you are the best known or even the best but it does mean you     บ
 บ  are smart and very good at what you do.  I also feel that if you act      บ
 บ  godly or feel godly then you are also not elite.  Just because you know   บ
 บ  big people or can do a few neat tricks with computers does not mean you   บ
 บ  are elite.  Elite is knowing you are smarter than the rest of the people  บ
 บ  and not calling them lame becasue they ask a dumb question.  If you are   บ
 บ  elite than you help them if they need help and you DO NOT act godly or    บ
 บ  show off.  You show people you are elite by doing what you know, not      บ
 บ  showing off or over using your powers.  That is what being elite is.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Undisclosed               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Undisclosed,                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Good letter, I agree that acting godly and trying to scare people     บ
 บ  shows just how un-elite you are.  If you laugh at someone because they    บ
 บ  don't know something, or cause you just think you are godlier you are     บ
 บ  not elite.  I know that I can get pissed and bitch at people for          บ
 บ  nothing, and make fun of new people, it is usually because I am stressed  บ
 บ  out and it helps the tension.  I only know of a few people I would        บ
 บ  consider actually elite.  One that stands out off hand is [Igor], the     บ
 บ  guy barely knows me, but has helped me with some sites and shit, and has  บ
 บ  never been a dick, although he could just tell people to piss off he      บ
 บ  doesn't.  Another easy way to tell if someone isn't elite is, if you see  บ
 บ  them saying shit like l337 or I'm leet, shit like that, usually just      บ
 บ  some guy who is seriously insecure about where he stands, this actually   บ
 บ  makes him look more like an idiot than anything else.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have a question for you and I was hoping that you might be able to  บ
 บ  answer.  I guess you could say that I am new to the scene, been around    บ
 บ  since november, and I have lately wanted to join a good group, as a       บ
 บ  courier, but all the big groups like Razor, RiSC, etc won't let you in    บ
 บ  unless you have some type of rep, or people know you in good #'s, you     บ
 บ  know what I mean?  My question is how are people like me supposed to      บ
 บ  obtain this rep if nobody is willing to help em?  I mean if I were to     บ
 บ  ask to be invited to a big #, my answer would be no, so I wouldn't get    บ
 บ  anywhere.  Well, thats all for now, and good job with the mag             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Bud                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Bud,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am not big on couriering, BUT I can tell you how some friends made  บ
 บ  it to groups not to long after starting in the scene.  The EASIEST way    บ
 บ  to get started, is to get a FAST shell, do that and you will have no      บ
 บ  problem leeching the newest shit from the fast couriers, THEN as soon as  บ
 บ  you get the shit on your shell, load up Phoenix (with fluffs of course)   บ
 บ  and start offering.  Sit in the decent channels like #Exceed or M8's      บ
 บ  warez channel.  Keep your shell in there as long as you can, offering     บ
 บ  the newest shit.  The groups do notice this and eventually you will get   บ
 บ  to know the good couriers and when you apply for a group they will help   บ
 บ  you out and tell the rest that you are decent.  By the way, there is one  บ
 บ  couriering group you should avoid trying to get into, I am not saying     บ
 บ  names because I don't need to start shit, BUT they have been around A     บ
 บ  LONNNNG time and they think they are the shit.  Most people find them     บ
 บ  amusing though, and a lot of their members are guys that just want        บ
 บ  another affiliation.  ALSO, if you look for the newer smaller groups      บ
 บ  they are happy to try out anyone at first and it is a good way to make    บ
 บ  contacts and get good experience.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* Happy couriering, and send me some sites!                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  How I do I know I'm 'leet ?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  You are an elite BBS SYSOP if...                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you have so many phone lines that you need a wallet to write      บ
 บ          them all down.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... your BBS is a HQ of so many groups that your login information    บ
 บ          takes a user 20 minutes to watch at with ISDN transfer.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... your telnet takes up 90% of the Internet bandwith.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you would have 200gigs of free HD space, if you didn't use 99%    บ
 บ          of it to hold the login- and phonenumbers-info.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  You are an elite COURIER if...                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you have your own supercomputer connected to ALL BBS systems      บ
 บ          around the globe simultaneously and it auto-copies every file     บ
 บ          uploaded somewhere to ALL others automatically.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you are idling on ALL channels in IRC at the same time, 24 hours  บ
 บ          a day.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... U.P.S. calles YOU when they need to carry somthing fast.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  You are an elite HACKER if...                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... the President will call YOU to press the red-button.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you have your own satilite in space.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you use space telescope hubble to make your passport photos.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... Compuserv has 20.000.000 accounts and all are faked by you.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... CNN calles YOU for news on the world.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... your IRC script does not only /kill nicks... it kills the         บ
 บ          bank-accounts of the specified person and writes him out for      บ
 บ          criminal investigation.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  You run an elite GROUP if...                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... you have more bots on IRC than members.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ... your pkzip'd *.nfo takes 1.3 MB alone.. and you pack it on every  บ
 บ          disk.                                                             บ

 บ      The following details your forecasts depending on your astrological   บ
 บ  sign.  Each sign designates your personal lucky numbers of the week.      บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Forecast for the week : The pressure is off as Mars transits into fun     บ
 บ  seeking Gemini.  It's not a time to slack, make changes instead.          บ
 บ  Compete in a different realm, try your hand at another art, you may find  บ
 บ  a new calling in the scene.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  <Aquarius> (January 20 to Feb 18) : You've found it!  The one warez       บ
 บ             package you've personally wanted for a long time, it may be    บ
 บ             larger than expected but who cares!  Grab a drink, go outside  บ
 บ             and relax while it downloads.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ           volunteered for and now can relax, though you were stressed out  บ
 บ           all night and had to get it done in just a few days, it pays     บ
 บ           off, while it may not be the best, you worked hard on it, and    บ
 บ           it will only get better from here on out.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aries> (March 21 to April 19) : You have a way of motivating others in   บ
 บ          your group, and those around you.  News comes from a close        บ
 บ          friend that may bring current projects to a halt.  Stick to it,   บ
 บ          and ride it out, you may be able to pull it off.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Taurus> (April 20 to May 20) : A hated enemy strikes a heavy blow, and   บ
 บ           a self-absorbed leader of yours gets cranky.  While things       บ
 บ           around you look bleak, turn to the ones that matter, your        บ
 บ           friends, while they are not the most popular, they will be       บ
 บ           there for you.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Gemini> (May 21 to June 21) : An associate pays back a long time favor,  บ
 บ           with an added bonus.  Fight the urge to give up on your          บ
 บ           projects unless you truly feel it is not giving you any          บ
 บ           satisfaction.  The help you have offered a new person leaves     บ
 บ           you with a sense of accomplishment, you have aided someone in    บ
 บ           need, and they will pay you back even if you feel it is not      บ
 บ           needed.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Cancer> (June 22 to July 22) : An uncommon chat with a person of power   บ
 บ           leaves you with a feeling of respect for him, you have computer  บ
 บ           trouble, OS acting up again, you decide to find a replacement,   บ
 บ           in the form of several files with a stupid code name for them.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Leo> (July 23 to August 22) : A friend nearby is destined to be your     บ
 บ        new partner, and in other areas of interest the ball starts         บ
 บ        rolling, look for new and exciting things to be happening soon,     บ
 บ        and make plans to be there to receive them.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Virgo> (August 23 to September 22) : Expect a generous offer for your    บ
 บ          skills in the very near future.  Your hard work pays off, and     บ
 บ          you may make it big if you play your cards right.  Look for an    บ
 บ          opening in a position you have wanted for a long time now, and    บ
 บ          go for it.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Libra> (September 23 to October 23) : You actually get outdoors this     บ
 บ          week, away from the computer and away from you room.  Enjoy it,   บ
 บ          and when you get back, you'll find your work easier to deal with  บ
 บ          if you take more time to get out more often.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Scorpio> (October 24 to November 21) : A material sign of prosperity is  บ
 บ            now affordable to you.  You impress the people around you with  บ
 บ            your dedication.  You become deeply involved in how stupid the  บ
 บ            word "cybersex" sounds and vow to blow up any such sites in     บ
 บ            the near future.                                                บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Xenon-Watch                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So you guys thought Rebel Chicken was bad?  Yeah, so did I.  I        บ
 บ  figured it just doesn't get any worse than him, he's a basket case!  I    บ
 บ  was wrong.  Early last week, Xenon called my house (we live just a few    บ
 บ  blocks away from each other) and said he wanted a bit of advice.  So      บ
 บ  there's this girl called Lisa that goes to our school, and there's this   บ
 บ  band that both Xenon and she like.  Of course, Xenon likes her just a     บ
 บ  tad more than he does the the band.  So he wanted to call her up and ask  บ
 บ  her out to the concert.  Welllll, not exactly.  He wanted to ask her out  บ
 บ  to go to a movie, alone, private, where he could show her what he's made  บ
 บ  of, but I'm sure he would have settled for a concert.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I asked him where he got this girl's phone number.  Obviously I was   บ
 บ  doubting that she actually GAVE it to him, God forbid.  So he laughed a   บ
 บ  bit, said I didn't REALLY want to know, and finally just as I was about   บ
 บ  to whack him, he told me.  Apparently he was house-sitting for the guy    บ
 บ  who went to the prom with this girl, and he thought he would do a little  บ
 บ  snooping around.  Actually, not so much that, he said the number was      บ
 บ  just there on a notepad and he couldn't resist.  Fair enough.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "So, genius.  What are you going to do when you're on the phone with  บ
 บ  her and she asks you where you got her number?"  "Oh... hehehehe"         บ
 บ  Hmm... I guess he didn't think of that.  Just as a side note, our school  บ
 บ  doesn't give out school directories, so it means the guys actually have   บ
 บ  to have some balls and get up and ask ... or they can just house-sit for  บ
 บ  the girl's boyfriend.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I don't generally mind it when I see Xenon completely humiliated, it  บ
 บ  happens quite a lot and is often the humor to my days, but this, this     บ
 บ  would majorly hurt.  And I still thought I could make it the humor of my  บ
 บ  day, so I wasn't going to lose anything.  I told him that I would call    บ
 บ  up Lisa's best friend, Erin, and ask her for the number.  And being that  บ
 บ  she IS Lisa's best friend, this could lead to some inside information.    บ
 บ  Sure, why not.  He agreed.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So the next evening, I called up Erin.  I told her I was doing a      บ
 บ  favor for a friend, that he's making me do this, and then I said "You     บ
 บ  know Xenon?"  I was quickly approached by a jumpy voice saying "NO I      บ
 บ  won't give Xenon Lisa's phone number!!!"  "Hahahaha, how did you know?!"  บ
 บ  I asked.  Apparently Lisa knew quite well, as did Erin, that Xenon liked  บ
 บ  her, and apparently she had warned Erin that she would kill her if she    บ
 บ  gave Xenon her number.  OUCH was all I could think.  I was really trying  บ
 บ  to restrain myself, I just said "Alright, well thanks, I had to ask ;-)"  บ
 บ  so she said "Heh, no problem."                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We hung up, and I must have been laughing for a good 5 minutes        บ
 บ  before I could put myself back together and call Xenon and tell him the   บ
 บ  news.  So, alas, we have found that Rebel Chicken is not the only one of  บ
 บ  his kind in this world, and apparently his partner in crime was right     บ
 บ  here the whole time.  So now I'm thinking "Is this a trend with all my    บ
 บ  friends?  Do I just tend to hang out with complete rejects?"  It's a      บ
 บ  scary thought.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Dark-Elf and Amy                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So apparently Rebel Chicken's letter to Emily inspired other young    บ
 บ  chickens (or Elves as the case may be) to write letters via email to      บ
 บ  THEIR girls, or girls-to-be.  Recently on IRC I had Dark-Elf online and   บ
 บ  he said he had just e-mailed this girl he really liked.  Well, that's     บ
 บ  legit.  Then, he asked me to publish it in RCN because he wanted to show  บ
 บ  his girl how famous he is.  Fair enough.  So here it is, the unedited,    บ
 บ  unabridged version. Enjoy.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Amy,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      How's your summer so far?  Mine has been good.  How has yours been    บ
 บ  so far? [Getting a tad repetitive here Dark!?]  Do you like school?  Or   บ
 บ  do you like going to school?  I like going to school because that's       บ
 บ  where all my friends are.  I liked being around you in school.  I miss    บ
 บ  being around you.  [Golly gee how sweet!]  Well so far this summer.  I    บ
 บ  went to the movies a couple times with my best friend, (Stephen).  I      บ
 บ  went to ultra-zone a lot.  I am a role-player at ultra-zone (I am proud)  บ
 บ  [well sure Dark, I would be too!].  Role-players are the best people at   บ
 บ  ultra-zone.  I have some good places.  We are going on vacation on July,  บ
 บ  4 1996.  We will be gone for 2 weeks to Florida.  Maybe we can go to the  บ
 บ  movies sometime.  We could just like meet there at the movie theatre.     บ
 บ  If you do not want to then don't.  Don't say yes because you can't say    บ
 บ  no [Dark, one thing you will find about women, is that they NEVER say     บ
 บ  Yes when they mean No!].  Say yes if you mean it.  If you know what I     บ
 บ  mean.  If you have a boyfriend now I shall understand.  Life's like a     บ
 บ  box of choclates [pffffft!!!].  You never know what you're going to get.  บ
 บ  Well this is a little guess into a box of choclates.  As to if you would  บ
 บ  like to spend some time with me [not original but kinda cute I guess!].   บ
 บ  If you don't wanna go to movies.  We can go to ultra-zone.  I shall       บ
 บ  protect you there [BUAAAAAAHAHAHAHA!!!].  It will be alot of fun for me   บ
 บ  wherever we go.  If you feel you are in commitment with that farmer guy   บ
 บ  [ooh, that may have cost you the medal right there!]?  Then don't go out  บ
 บ  with me. Especially a person I don not even know.  This letter was        บ
 บ  semi-hard to write, because I did not know the out come of the            บ
 บ  reader(You).  I tried to give it to you in school but I could not [cuz    บ
 บ  I'm a whimp].  All these mixed emotions!  It's hard being a TeenAge boy   บ
 บ  [HAHAHAHAAH!!!].  Please don't show this letter to anyone [hmm.. now I'm  บ
 บ  confused].  If you ask me if you can show it to them then I shall give    บ
 บ  ya an answer.  If PJ wants to read it she can (she is your best friend).  บ
 บ  She really does not like me as a friend though.  I just think me and PJ   บ
 บ  think differently.  Just wanted her know that.  Remember.  You mean Yes   บ
 บ  or You mean No.  Gimme an answer tha'ts in your heart for there is an     บ
 บ  answer to any question in the universe. [roo!?]                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The time is 1:43am 6-20-96.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I write things real late because tha'ts when all my feelings come     บ
 บ  out.  I usually go to sleep earlier though.  Hope you feel the same way   บ
 บ  I do about you as you do me [see comments below!].  If you don't then     บ
 บ  say now.  It will be ok.  If you do please tell me.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Love,                        บ
 บ                                                  Dark-Elf                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My my my... MYYYYY my my.  MYYYYYYYYYYY my my my!  Well Dark-Elf, I   บ
 บ  really hope for the best.  Hope being the key word in that sentence.  So  บ
 บ  I have a few things to say.  First of all, how the FUCK are you going to  บ
 บ  "protect" Amy at ultra-zone!?  Second, what IS ultra-zone!?  Third, next  บ
 บ  time you write a girl a letter, run it through one of the RCN Editors     บ
 บ  first, we'll fix all the grammar ;-).  And lastly, let me just comment    บ
 บ  on the sentence "Hope you feel the same way I do about you as you do      บ
 บ  me."  There's a very important thing when writing a letter to a girl for  บ
 บ  the first time.  You HAVE to make sure that the romantic part of the      บ
 บ  letter says exactly what you meant for it to say.  The small-talk         บ
 บ  doesn't matter too much, it just burns space on the paper, it's the       บ
 บ  leading action, but your climax can't say something you didn't mean for   บ
 บ  it to.  Let me first explain what that sentence means, in reality.  It    บ
 บ  means that you hope she feels the same things you feel for her as she     บ
 บ  "does" your or, as your average girl would understand, as she has sex     บ
 บ  with you.  My my my, on a first letter, this is NOT what you want to      บ
 บ  say!  So next time, write something more to the effect of "I hope you     บ
 บ  feel the same way about me as I feel about you."  Anyway, good luck, and  บ
 บ  remember, our thoughts are with you.  Uh oh.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Anonymous                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : Jimmy and Rape                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      One day Jimmy was sitting on IRC talking to some chick.  He didn't    บ
 บ  know what this would lead to.  Jimmy always being a warez man, never      บ
 บ  hung out much in the sex rooms.  One day Jimmy decided to mozy on down    บ
 บ  into #Sex and maybe take it over or do something.  But as he walked in    บ
 บ  he noticed Britany sitting there talking bout her large sites and big     บ
 บ  connections.  This immediately attracted Jimmy to Britany. They began to  บ
 บ  talk about his long membership to his group and her gloating about her    บ
 บ  big connections.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      These two got along fine, until one day when Jimmy stole her shell.   บ
 บ  Britany has never let anyone use her shell, so she kinda felt violated.   บ
 บ  She started crying, she started screaming, "I told him to stop, but he    บ
 บ  kept on using it.. over and over.."  Finally he was done with the shell   บ
 บ  and threw it like a dirty old rag.  He never did talk to Britany again.   บ
 บ  Until one day Jimmy got summoned to court.  Britany claims she was        บ
 บ  seduced into giving him her shell and he took advantage of her.  Jimmy    บ
 บ  said she wanted it.  She knew she wanted me to use her shell.  In the     บ
 บ  end Jimmy ended up in jail for shell raping.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
